***лесть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лесть.html>лесть</a> (13857)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">льсть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lĭstĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. According to Vasmer, a link with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">List</i> is possible.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесть.html>лесть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lestʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесть.html>ле́сти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесть.html>ле́сти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесть.html>ле́стей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>flattery, adulation, cajolery</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лестный.html>ле́стный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">léstnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:летальный.html>лета́льный</a> (23293)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">letal</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летальный.html>лета́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">letálʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)лета́льнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)лета́льней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lethal</li></ol>

***летать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a> (1990)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lětati</i>, frequentative from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*letěti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">letátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полетать.html>полета́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полетать.html>полета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poletátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, are abstract verbs. Their counterparts, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полететь.html>полете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poletétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are Russian concrete verbs.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i>See <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for derived terms.</i></li></ul>

***лететь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лететь</a> (1021)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">летѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letěti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*letěti</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">letétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полететь.html>полете́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly, to be flying</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полететь.html>полете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poletétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are Russian concrete verbs. Their counterparts, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полетать.html>полета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poletátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, are abstract verbs.
</p>

***лето.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>ле́то</a> (877)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěto</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">year</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*leh₁tom</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">літо</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lito</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">слеціць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sljecicʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to warm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">слетный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sljetnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">warmish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">лято</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljato</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh"><a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>ле́то</a></i>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">љето</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">poletje</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">léto</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">leto</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">lato</i>, and Upper and Lower Sorbian <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">lěto</i>. Possibly also cognate with Old Gutnish <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">laþigs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and dialectal Swedish <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">låding</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">låing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">i lådigs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">last spring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from Proto-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lēþ-</i>), and with Irish <i class="Latn mention" lang="ga">lá</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">day</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. In addition, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">лѣто</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lěto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> may be related to Old Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">лѣѭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lějǫ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which is cognate with Lithuanian and Latvian <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">lietus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Possibly also related to Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">laetus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rich, fertile, excellent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>ле́то</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">léto</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>ле́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лета́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>summer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>ле́том</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>létom</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in summer; in the summer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>ле́то</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>léto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">for the summer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прошлый.html>про́шлое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>ле́то</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">próšloje <b>léto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">last summer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>: years, age, summers
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pjatʹ <b>let</b> tomú nazád</i> ― <span class="e-translation">five years ago</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лета́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On v <b>letáx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is elderly.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Skólʹko vam <b>let</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How old are you?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:летописец.html>летопи́сец</a> (18960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Shansky and Zhuravlyov, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χρονογράφος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khronográphos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chronicler, annalist</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">time-writer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>ле́то</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">léto</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">year</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to write</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ец</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летописец.html>летопи́сец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">letopísec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летописец.html>летопи́сца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летописец.html>летопи́сцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летописец.html>летопи́сцев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chronicler, annalist</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chronicle</li></ol>

***летопись.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:летопись.html>ле́топись</a> (14554)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Back-formation from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летописец.html>летопи́сец</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letopísec</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chronicler, annalist</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (per Shansky and Zhuravlev). For the initial stress, compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:живопись.html>жи́вопись</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žívopisʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надпись.html>на́дпись</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nádpisʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подпись.html>по́дпись</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pódpisʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запись.html>за́пись</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zápisʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, etc.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летопись.html>ле́топись</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">létopisʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летопись.html>ле́тописи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летопись.html>ле́тописи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летопись.html>ле́тописей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="Russian-a_relation_of_events">annals, chronicle, record, fasti <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a relation of events</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a relation of events</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">анна́лы</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">annály</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хроника.html>хро́ника</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xrónika</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-účij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летучий.html>лету́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">letúčij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>flying</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shifting</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> volatile</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лечить.html>ле́чащий</a> (3233)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечить.html>ле́чащий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">léčaščij</span>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечить.html>лечи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lečítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***лечение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лечение.html>лече́ние</a> (1174)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечить.html>лечи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lečítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечение.html>лече́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lečénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечение.html>лече́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечение.html>лече́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечение.html>лече́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>treatment, cure</li></ol>

***лечиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лечиться.html>лечи́ться</a> (6995)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечить.html>лечи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lečítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечиться.html>лечи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lečítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to take treatment, to receive treatment undergo a cure <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a patient</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лечиться.html>лечи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> чего́-л</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lečítʹsja</b> ot čevó-l</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to receive treatment for smth</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лечиться.html>лечи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lečítʹsja</b> grjázjami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take/undergo a mud cure</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лечиться.html>лечи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самому</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lečítʹsja</b> samomu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to doctor oneself</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лечиться.html>ле́читесь</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u kovó vy <b>léčitesʹ</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">who is your doctor?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cure <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a disease</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лечиться.html>ле́чится</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éta boléznʹ dólgo <b>léčitsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this disease takes long to cure</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лечиться.html>ле́чится</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éta boléznʹ ne <b>léčitsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is no cure for this disease</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to heal <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of wounds, burns</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ожог.html>ожо́ги</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лечиться.html>ле́чатся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ožógi <b>léčatsja</b> dólgo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">burns heal slowly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечить.html>лечи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lečítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***лечь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лечь</a> (1229)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*leťi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лечь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lečʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложиться.html>ложи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lie down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лечь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кость.html>костьми́</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lečʹ</b> kostʹmí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall in battle, to do one's damnedest, to go all out</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лечь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совесть.html>со́весть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lečʹ</b> na sóvestʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to weigh on one's conscience</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лечь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:основа.html>осно́ву</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lečʹ</b> v osnóvu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to underlie</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лечь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:больница.html>больни́цу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lečʹ</b> v bolʹnícu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go to hospital (to be hospitalised)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лечь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спать</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lečʹ</b> spatʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go to bed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fall, to cover <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of snow etc. on the ground</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to flow <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of paint being applied to a surface</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to heave <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to move in a certain direction or into a certain situation</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лечь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрейф.html>дрейф</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">idiomatic<span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> nautical</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lečʹ</b> v drejf</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lie to, to heave to</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall over, to die</li></ol>

***леший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:леший.html>ле́ший</a> (9196)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěšь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěsъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">forest, woods</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-jь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">possessive suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Leshy_%281906%29.jpg/220px-Leshy_%281906%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="186" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Leshy_%281906%29.jpg/330px-Leshy_%281906%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Leshy_%281906%29.jpg/440px-Leshy_%281906%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="638" data-file-height="539" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:леший.html>ле́ший</a></div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:леший.html>ле́ший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">léšij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:леший.html>ле́шего</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:леший.html>ле́шие</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:леший.html>ле́ших</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> leshy (<i>a male woodland spirit in Slavic mythology who protects wild animals and forests</i>)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лещ.html>лещ</a> (15878)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лещ.html>лещ</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lešč</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лещ.html>леща́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лещ.html>лещи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лещ.html>леще́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bream</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> slap in the face, box on the ear</li></ol>

***ли.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> (88)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle_3">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">li</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative particle<span class="ib-comma">,</span> placed after the first word in a sentence or phrase</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Do/does/did...? Is/are/was/were...?
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ете</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Znájete <b>li</b> vy?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Do</b> you know?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Xorošó <b>li</b> jemú?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Is</b> he okay?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отправить.html>отпра́вил</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:письмо.html>письмо́</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Otprávil <b>li</b> ja pisʹmó?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Did</b> I send the letter?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">li</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>whether, if</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The subordinate clause with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></b> expresses an occurrence (i.e., an event, incident, news, or rumor) that happened in the past or that could possibly happen in the future. In this specific case, the main clause shows confirming or denying the occurrence (as described in the subordinate clause with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></b>). For example:</li></ul>
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>Они</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спросить.html>спро́сят</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отдыхать.html>отдыха́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> Андрей раньше</b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oni sprosjat, <b>otdyxal li Andrej ranʹše</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They will ask <b>if Andrei has been on a holiday before</b>.</span></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd>(The subordinate clause is an occurrence that happened in the past.)</dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>ска́жет</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:остаться.html>оста́нется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дома</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On ne skažet, <b>ostanetsja li on doma</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He will not say <b>if he will stay home</b>.</span></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd>(The subject of the main clause and the subordinate clause denotes the same person "he". The subordinate clause is an occurrence that could possibly happen in the future.)</dd></dl></dd>
<dd>The main clause often has a verb that describes an occurrence, such as verbs pertaining to asking or talking. And also, depending on the context, the subordinate clause with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></b> could be regarded as indirect speech.</dd></dl>
<ul><li>To make a sentence that expresses curiosity about a topic while using <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></b> in the subordinate clause, <b><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интересно.html>интере́сно</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">interésno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ....</b> is often used for the main clause. For example:</li></ul>
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b>(<a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:интересно.html>интере́сно</a>,</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тусовка.html>тусо́вке</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>(Mne) interesno,</b> budet li ona na tusovke.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<b>(I) am interested (wonder)</b> if she will be at the party.</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вызвать.html>вы́звала</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такси.html>такси́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:выйти.html>вы́шла</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>нашла́</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чуть.html>чуть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:увести.html>увели́</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:представлять.html>Представля́ешь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:парень.html>па́рень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:интересоваться.html>интересу́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такси.html>такси́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говорю́</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:машинка.html>маши́нка</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja vyzvala taksi, vyšla, našla - a jeje čutʹ ne uveli! Predstavljaješʹ, uže stoit parenʹ i <b>interesujetsja ne jevo li taksi</b> ja govorju - moja mašinka!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I called a taxi, went outside, found it and my ride was almost stolen! Guess what, a guy had already been there and <b>wondering if</b> that was his cab. I said "that's my cab!"</span></div></li></ul></dd></dl>
<ul><li>To make a sentence that expresses doubt about a topic while using <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></b> in the subordinate clause, <b>(SUB) <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne znatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ....</b>, <b>(SUB) <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помнить.html>помни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne pomnitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ....</b>, <b>(SUB) <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сомневаться.html>сомнева́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">somnevátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ....</b>, and <b><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трудно.html>тру́дно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Trúdno skazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ....</b> are often used for the main clause. For example:</li></ul>
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a>,</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дедушка.html>де́душка</a> по-арабски.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ja ne znaju,</b> govorit li moj deduška po-arabski.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>I don't know</b> if my grandfather speaks Arabic.</span></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd>(The main clause shows a doubtful attitude by not knowing whether the old man speaks Arabic.)</dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помнить.html>помню</a>,</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:выключить.html>вы́ключил</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:телевизор.html>телеви́зор</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ja ne pomnju,</b> vyključil li ja televizor.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>I don't remember</b> if I turned off the television.</span></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd>(The main clause shows a doubtful attitude by not remembering whether the television is turned off.)</dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сомневаться.html>сомнева́юсь</a>,</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сигарета.html>сигаре́ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ja somnevajusʹ,</b> kuril li ja sigarety často.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>I doubt</b> that I smoked cigarettes often.</span></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd>(The main clause shows a doubtful attitude by being skeptical about the smoking habit in the past.)</dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трудно.html>Тру́дно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a>,</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:понять.html>пойму́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> волонтёры <a href = vnd.unilang:установка.html>устано́вки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задание.html>зада́ния</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Trudno skazatʹ,</b> pojmut li volontjóry ustanovki etovo zadanija.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>It's difficult to tell</b> that the volunteers understand the guidelines of this task.'</span></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd>(The main clause shows a doubtful attitude by having a difficulty of explaining about the volunteers' situation.)</dd></dl></dd></dl>

***либо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:либо.html>ли́бо</a> (458)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">li</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ибо.html>и́бо</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">íbo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:ибо.html>и́бо</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ibo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">for, because</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">i</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">бо</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">because</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:либо.html>ли́бо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">líbo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>either...or
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:либо.html>ли́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:либо.html>ли́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>líbo</b> ja, <b>líbo</b> on</i> ― <span class="e-translation">either I or he</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:либо.html>ли́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:либо.html>ли́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>líbo</b> odín, <b>líbo</b> drugój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">either one or the other</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">íli</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:союз.html>Сою́з</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
